<script>function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
  if (!cookieName || document.cookie.indexOf(cookieName) === -1) {
    return undefined;
  }

  try {
    var cookieArray = document.cookie.match(new RegExp("(^| )".concat(cookieName, "=([^;]+)")));

    if (cookieArray && cookieArray.length > 0) {
      return decodeURIComponent(cookieArray.pop());
    }

    return undefined;
  } catch (e) {
    return undefined;
  }
}; function getCustomerNameAndGreeting() {
  var isSignedIn = getCookieValue("hasCID") === "1";
  var customer = getCookieValue("customer");

  if (isSignedIn && customer && customer.length) {
    try {
      customer = JSON.parse(customer);

      if (customer.firstName) {
        return "Hi, ".concat(customer.firstName, " ").concat(customer.lastNameInitial);
      }

      return undefined;
    } catch (e) {
      return undefined;
    }
  }

  return undefined;
}; function replaceAccountSubLinkText() {
  var customerNameAndGreeting = getCustomerNameAndGreeting();
  var accountSubText = document.querySelector("#signIn");

  if (customerNameAndGreeting && accountSubText) {
    accountSubText.textContent = customerNameAndGreeting;
  }
};
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () { 
      try{
        replaceAccountSubLinkText();
      } catch(e) {console.log("Error in glass-hf client code", e)}
    });
</script>

class="SeoCustomHtml-data"><h2>Walmart for Business</h2><p>Running your own business not only requires a lot of work but also a significant amount of supplies. Thankfully, you can get everything you need in one place at Walmart.com.</p><p>If you're starting a small business there are a variety of one-time purchases you will have to make upfront like office furniture and electronics. Make sure that you and your employees have a desk and office chair along with the appropriate <a href="https://www.walmart.com/browse/home/file-cabinets/4044_103150_97116_132967">filing cabinets</a> and storage. Another smart investment is an all-in-one printer that has the ability to fax, scan, print and copy. You'll also need an array of office basics including <a href="https://www.walmart.com/browse/office/scissors/1229749_1046059_5872960_6778521">scissors</a>, staplers, pens and sticky notes.</p><p>As a business owner there will be a number of items you need on a monthly basis like <a href="https://www.walmart.com/browse/office/paper/1229749_6562796">paper</a>, ink cartridges, paper clips, shipping materials and cleaning supplies. Save money by taking advantage of Walmart's free 2-day shipping on all the items you need to keep your office or business running smoothly, month after month. Be sure to also take advantage of other Walmart services like check cashing.</p><p>At Walmart, you can even stock your break room with paper <a href="https://www.walmart.com/c/kp/dinner-plate-sets">plates</a>, <a href="https://www.walmart.com/browse/household-essentials/paper-towels-napkins/1115193_1073264_1149383">napkins</a> and garbage bags all at Every Day Low Prices. Save money. <script>(function() {
  function getCookie(name) {
    if (name) {
      var cookieRegex = new RegExp(name + "=([^\\s;]*)");
      var sMatch = document.cookie.match(cookieRegex);
      if (sMatch && sMatch[1]) {
        return decodeURIComponent(sMatch[1]);
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  function get(path, obj) {
    try {
      var val;
      var paths = typeof path === "string" ? path.split(".") : path;
      if (obj && typeof obj === "object") {
        paths.forEach(function(k, i) {
          if (i === 0) {
            val = obj[k];
          } else if (val) {
            val = val[k];
          }
        });
      }
      return val;
    } catch (e) {
      // In case of an error, prevents side effects on page level
      return;
    }
  }

  function getAppName() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.applicationName", window);
  }

  function getMidasConfig() {
    return get("_wml.config.ccm.midasConfig", window) || {};
  }
  function getMidasUiConfig() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.midasConfig", window) || {};
  }

  function getMidasCfgVal(cfgName) {
    var cfg = getMidasConfig();
    var appName = getAppName();
    var pageCfgKey = appName + "-" + cfgName;
    return cfg[pageCfgKey] || cfg[cfgName];
  }

  function loadScript(scriptUrl) {
    var script = document.createElement("script");
    script.async = true;
    script.src = scriptUrl;
    document.head.appendChild(script);
  }

  function loadAds() {
    if (!loadAds.loaded) {
      addPerfMark("load-midas-display");
      loadAds.loaded = true;
      var displayAds = getMidasCfgVal("displayAds") !== "false";
      if (displayAds) {
        var MDABT = getCookie("MDABT");
        var midasDisplayScript =
          getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABT) ||
          getMidasCfgVal("midasDisplayScript");
        var gptUrl = "//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js";
        if (getMidasCfgVal("loadDisplayScript") !== "false") {
          loadScript(midasDisplayScript);
        }
        loadScript(gptUrl);
      }
    }
  }

  function loadS2SScripts() {
    if (!loadS2SScripts.loaded) {
      addPerfMark("load-s2s-midas-scripts");
      loadS2SScripts.loaded = true;
      var MDABTS2S = getCookie("MDABTS2S");
      var midasS2SScript =
        getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABTS2S) || getMidasCfgVal("midasS2SScript");
      loadScript(midasS2SScript);
    }
  }

  function addPerfMark(markName){
    var hasPerfMark = !!get("performance.mark", window);
    if (hasPerfMark) {
      // For some reason it causes an error when you store the reference of the mark fn.
      window.performance.mark(markName);
    }
  }
  var loadS2SEvent =
    getCookie("loadS2SEvent") ||
    getMidasUiConfig()["loadS2SEvent"] ||
    getMidasCfgVal("loadS2SEvent") ||
    "hasS2SPayload";

  var loadEvent =
    getCookie("loadEvent") ||
    getMidasUiConfig()["loadEvent"] ||
    getMidasCfgVal("loadEvent") ||
    "instant";
  window._wml.adLoader = (function() {
    var eventListeners = {};
    return {
      fireEvent: function fireEvent(eventName) {
        addPerfMark('fire-event-' + eventName);
        var listeners = eventListeners[eventName];

        if (listeners) {
          listeners.forEach(function(listener) {
            listener();
          });
        }
      },
      subscribe: function subscribe(eventName, listener) {
        if (!eventListeners[eventName]) {
          eventListeners[eventName] = [];
        }

        eventListeners[eventName].push(listener);
      },
    };
  })();

  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadEvent, loadAds);
  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadS2SEvent, loadS2SScripts);
  _wml.adLoader.fireEvent("instant"); // Default load ads immediately
})();

var applicationName = _wml.config.ui.applicationName || "default";

  _wml.config.ccm.midasConfig.wpa &&
  _wml.config.ccm.midasConfig.wpa !== "false"
);
